# Design Coverage Manifest

Every concrete deliverable from `DESIGN.md`, mapped to the phase it lands in and its current status.

**Status legend**:
- ‚úÖ **DONE** ‚Äî fully implemented and verified
- üü° **PARTIAL** ‚Äî data/scaffolding exists, behavior pending later phase
- ‚è≥ **PENDING** ‚Äî not started, scheduled
- üí≠ **OPEN** ‚Äî open-ended ("many more X" ‚Äî track count over time)

**Phase exit ritual** (what I MUST do before declaring a phase complete):
1. Read this file end-to-end.
2. For every row tagged with the current phase, verify status against the codebase.
3. If anything tagged for this phase is still PENDING or PARTIAL, fix it or explicitly defer with the user's approval before marking the phase complete.
4. Update statuses in this file whenever a row's state changes.

Rows flipped to ‚úÖ: kr-nemesis-return / -taunt / -final, kr-response-inquisition / -pantheon / -allstars. **REMAINING**: kr-act-scaling balance tuning (wants playtest data ‚Äî don't guess) + a full validation playthrough. Prior audit:** 2026-05-28 (**Spectra fleshed out from teaser to full companion + new `flawless_reign` achievement.** Sixth fully-built companion landed: ghost-girl otaku with 113 sprites baked under 66 semantic expression IDs, runtime variant rotation, 25% ghost-flicker opacity overlay, 627-line dialogue bank covering all categories + 100% specifics. Prior audit:** 2026-05-26 (**Achievements popup conversion + leaderboard view overhaul + legendary toast pass.** Big visual + structural pass driven by user iteration through this session. Twelve new Section 41 rows landed, all ‚úÖ DONE: **`ach-popup-conversion`** ‚Äî AchievementsOverlay converted from a full-screen panel to a centered popup using the shared `Overlay` shell (1300√ó840, gold accent, unfurl animation), matching `LeaderboardOverlay`'s dimensions so the two read as sibling Hall-of-X popups. `_render` ‚Üí `_renderBody` returns just inner content; the shell provides backdrop + close X + Esc + backdrop-click. Header z-index bumped to 20 so the title-picker dropdown paints above tabs/recent/view-wrap. Title centered in the shell's header bar via `:has(.qf-ach)` selector ‚Äî scoped so other overlays keep their left-aligned titles. Grid forced to 3 columns with `repeat(3, minmax(0, 1fr))` (the canonical fix for unequal CSS grid columns when one card has a wider non-wrapping chip). View-wrap padding bumped to 24px each side to clear the shell's ~18px inset gold frame. **`ach-reward-aware-icons`** ‚Äî icon medal color driven by `data-reward-type` (boss/companion/title/recognition) instead of category. Pure-recognition cards get cream icons; reward-bearing cards adopt their reward chip's color. Creates a per-card two-tone read ‚Äî colored border (category) √ó colored medal (reward type). With the move to emoji icons (next row), the icon glyph itself uses OS-native emoji colors, but the icon badge BORDER still inherits the reward-type color so the signal isn't lost. **`ach-lb-podium-rich`** ‚Äî achievement leaderboard's podium upgraded from simple [badge + name + count] to the FULL triptych matching the main run-leaderboard: [companion sprite \| floating #N badge + boss portrait + player name + title chip + trophy count \| stats block]. DOM order `[#2, #1, #3]` with `1fr 1.2fr 1fr` columns + `align-items: end` so cards step UPWARD in a proper podium silhouette (200/170/140px heights). Companion sprite + boss portrait + active-title chip all gracefully degrade for rows that predate those fields. `_loadLeaderboard` extended to extract companionId/bossLevel/days/kills/activeTitle. **`ach-lb-achievement-stats`** ‚Äî podium stats block content rewritten from RUN stats (BOSS LV / DAYS / KILLS ‚Äî wrong context) to achievement-derived TITLES / BOSSES / COMPANIONS counts decoded from `achievementBits`, color-coded by reward type. Totals reflect "total ACCESS" (starters + achievement-unlocked) ‚Äî BOSSES = 3 starters + X / 12 total, COMPANIONS = 3 starters + X / 4 total. **`ach-lb-trophy-block`** ‚Äî headline trophy count upgraded from plain text to a styled block with rank-colored big number (28/22/20px per rank), soft glow, smaller denominator, and a 5px progress bar showing % unlocked. **`ach-lb-empty-state`** ‚Äî YOUR-RANK band always renders even when the leaderboard is empty so the player sees their own count regardless of remote data; mango shows "EXCLUDED (CHEAT)" in the band; context-aware empty message explains why the board is empty for mango. **`ach-lb-placeholder-podium`** ‚Äî podium ALWAYS renders 3 slots; missing ranks show inert "AWAITING CHALLENGER" placeholders so the layout doesn't read broken on sparse boards. **`ach-lb-global-stats`** ‚Äî new stats panel below the ranked list (TOTAL KEEPERS / AVG TROPHIES / RAREST TROPHY / MOST POPULAR TITLE) computed from in-memory data, fills the dead zone below sparse boards + adds permanent global context. **`ach-lb-viewer-leaderboard-hide`** ‚Äî LEADERBOARD destination button hidden in viewer mode (drilled into another player's grid) ‚Äî avoids confusing nesting + frees the slot for the COMPARE WITH YOU toggle. **`ach-compare-toggle-inline`** ‚Äî compare toggle moved from `position: absolute; top: 30px; right: 24px` (a relic of the full-screen layout that put it on top of the LEADERBOARD button) to inline flow in the header. **`ach-legendary-toast`** ‚Äî legendary unlocks (the 6 hand-picked `def.legendary: true` achievements) get a tier-aware toast: RARE TROPHY eyebrow, "LEGENDARY UNLOCKED" header, gold-bright frame with ember inset glow + 2.2s pulse, larger glyph + title, 10s dwell, plus a 22-particle gold burst fountaining leftward into the play area (CSS-keyframed, per-particle `--dx/--dy` trajectory vars, biased to a 120¬∞ leftward arc since the toast sits on the right edge of the HUD). Legendary tier is now data-driven via `def.legendary` in `achievements.json` ‚Äî the JS reads the same flag for both grid card shimmer and toast tier branching. **`ach-title-picker-cleanup`** ‚Äî HIGH-severity bug found in audit: title-picker outside-click handler was leaking when the player closed the overlay while picker was open. Centralized teardown in `_onOverlayClose` (now the Overlay shell's onClose callback) tears down keydown + outside-click + nested viewer in one path. Also updated the visual-polish row's notes to reflect post-feedback iterations: padding-right on the card-col for rarity badge gutter; reward-chip nowrap with ellipsis; name color reverted to parchment cream so each card has ONE focal point (the icon medal) instead of three competing same-color elements; thematic emoji icons with U+FE0F variation selectors forcing emoji presentation on glyphs that default to monochrome. Previous audit 2026-05-26 (**Per-name storage refactor + achievements visual polish pass.** Driven by user feedback that LJ saw mango's "all unlocked" state ‚Äî all player-progress keys were globally-scoped, so mango's cheat writes leaked into every other account. Refactored every key to per-name (`<base>:<trimmed-name>`) matching the existing `maxBossLevel` pattern: `qf.companions.unlocked`, `qf.achievements.unlocked`, `qf.achievements.metrics`, `qf.player.titles`, `qf.achievements.timestamps`, `qf.player.active_title_id`. Legacy global keys wiped at module load (Option A ‚Äî no production data to migrate). `PlayerProfile.setName()` emits `NAME_CHANGED` so `AchievementSystem._reloadForCurrentPlayer()` re-hydrates without a page refresh. Mango cheat now writes only to mango's slot. Earlier the same day: visual polish pass on the achievements overlay (`ach-visual-polish` row) ‚Äî per-category color tokens, reward-chip semantic colors, subtle card-bg tints, title chip inherits source-category color, legendary-tier shimmer treatment for 6 hand-picked endgame achievements, per-achievement icon variety in `achievements.json`. Previous audit 2026-05-25 (**Section 41 ‚Äî title selection + recent unlocks + leaderboard title display.** Three new rows ‚úÖ DONE: (1) **`ach-title-selection`** ‚Äî the active-title chip in the AchievementsOverlay header is now clickable; clicking drops a floating picker beneath with one row per unlocked title plus an `‚óá AUTO` option that clears the pin and resumes most-recently-unlocked auto-promotion. Persisted under new `qf.profile.activeTitleId` localStorage key (`null` = AUTO). `PlayerProfile.getActiveTitle()` now prefers the selected id and falls back to most-recent. Picker is absolutely positioned against `.qf-ach` so opening it doesn't push the header; outside-click closes it; selection patches the chip name in-place. (2) **`ach-recent-strip`** ‚Äî RECENT UNLOCKS strip between the tabs row and the grid in self-view, showing the 3 most-recent unlocks with relative-time labels ("12 minutes ago" / "Just now"). Driven by new `qf.achievements.timestamps` localStorage key (written by `PlayerProfile.unlockAchievement`; retroactive scan timestamps back-fill on first boot). Auto-hidden when the player has zero unlocks; viewer mode skips it (no timestamp feed for other players). (3) **`ach-lb-title-display`** ‚Äî active title shown on the main run-leaderboard in place of the legacy IMMORTAL / BUTCHER / CUNNING accolades. Plumbed via `meta.active_title` on the run payload; LeaderboardOverlay's `_normalize` reads it into `row.title`; podium + detail chips render `title \|\| accolade` so older rows without the field keep the legacy top-3 labels (back-compat). Chip CSS got `max-width: 160/220px` + ellipsis because the longest title is "Veteran Exterminator" (20 chars). Previous audit 2026-05-25 (**Section 41 polish + deferral close-out.** Five row additions, all ‚úÖ DONE: (1) **`ach-titles`** ‚Äî title-reward system. 17 high-tier achievements (10 boss-level 11‚Äì20 + 7 mastery / cumulative-grind) now grant a player title via a new `title` field on the achievement definition. `PlayerProfile.unlockTitle/getUnlockedTitles/getActiveTitle` persist them under `qf.player.titles`; active title auto-promotes to the most-recently-unlocked one. Surfaced as a gold-burst `‚ú¶ TITLE ¬∑ <name>` chip in the AchievementsOverlay header (self-view only). Title-granting cards show a `‚ú¶ Title: <name>` reward chip. (2) **`ach-true-approach-a`** ‚Äî boss-archetype unlocks now go through `PlayerProfile.isAchievementUnlocked(boss-level-achId)` instead of `maxBossLevel >=` direct reads. ArchetypeSelect's UNLOCK_GATES maps each archetype to its achievement id (e.g. golem ‚Üî rising_power). Existing players see zero behaviour change because the retroactive scan unlocks the matching achievements on first boot. Cleaner architectural promise ‚Äî bosses unlock when their achievement unlocks. (3) **`ach-toast-batching`** ‚Äî `AchievementSystem._retroactiveScan` now does a two-pass scan: collect all unlockable achievements without firing, then queue them via setTimeout with 900ms initial delay + 700ms stagger so existing high-progress players don't get their toasts silently dropped by the ToastQueue MAX_TOASTS=4 cap. (4) **`ach-rarity`** ‚Äî client-side per-achievement rarity stats. Leaderboard fetch is now eager on overlay-open (was lazy until LB tab activated); ingested rows feed `AchievementSystem.ingestRarityFromRows` which computes how many players have each achievement. Cards get a small top-right badge: "5% rare" (gold-bright) for <10%, "earned" (muted) otherwise. Sample size kept alongside fraction for future tooltips. (5) **`ach-class-hunter-tune`** ‚Äî Class Hunter target 9 ‚Üí 11 to match the count of regularly-spawnable classes in `adventurerClasses.json`. Description tightened. (1) **Streak** ‚Äî `streak` category; the Director tracks consecutive full-party-wipe days (`_wipedToday` set on `KNOWLEDGE_PARTY_WIPED`, evaluated on `DAY_PHASE_ENDED`) and calls out milestones 3/5/8/12/20/30. (3) **Per-archetype-ability reactions** ‚Äî 8 `arch_*` categories wired to 9 signature-ability events (`GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_FIRED`, `DEMON_SACRIFICE_FIRED`, `DEMON_HELLGATE_SPAWNED`, `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_FIRED`, `VAMPIRE_CHARM_MARKED` + `SUCCUBUS_CHARM_APPLIED` ‚Üí shared `arch_charm`, `GNOLL_HUNTERS_PACK_REFILLED`, `MYCONID_SPORE_DAY_BEGAN`, `WRAITH_HAUNT_SPAWNED`); high-frequency per-hit/per-tick archetype events deliberately excluded so she doesn't machine-gun. ## 1b. Monster boss redesign ‚Äî supersedes the 15-archetype system (target: 10 monster bosses)

> See DESIGN.md ‚Üí "Monster boss redesign" for the locked spec per boss (one-or-two playstyle-defining abilities; no padding modifiers).
> Spec finalized 2026-05-02. Implementation in progress ‚Äî order is `1b.1` (Orc) ‚Üí `1b.11` (Gnoll), ascending complexity / shared-infra dependencies.

| ID | Boss | Locked abilities (headline summary) | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| orc         | Orc Veteran      | **Loot the Fallen** ‚Äî each orc keeps +1 ATK per kill (per-orc, lost on death). **Warband** ‚Äî orcs in the same room give every other orc in that room +5% ATK and +5% DEF, stacks per ally, no cap. | 1b.1 / 1b.12 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-02 ‚Äî both abilities) | **Loot the Fallen (1b.1):** `BossArchetypeSystem` listens for `ADVENTURER_DIED`/`MINION_DIED` while archetype = orc + killer is an orc-tagged minion; bumps `lootAtkBonus` (no longer writes `stats.attack` directly ‚Äî Warband's recompute owns the live value). On death, `lootAtkBonus` is zeroed; the next `_tickOrc` pass auto-rebalances the cluster. `MinionRenderer` paints a small "+N" badge in orc-red at the bottom-left of the orc sprite (gated by archetype + tag + bonus>0). **Warband (1b.12):** `_tickOrc` runs every frame from `tick(delta)` for the orc archetype. Per orc, looks up its current room via `dungeonGrid.getRoomAtTile`, counts other live orc-tagged minions in the same room, derives `atkMult = 1 + allies √ó ORC_WARBAND_ATK_PCT_PER_ALLY` (0.05) and `defMult = 1 + allies √ó ORC_WARBAND_DEF_PCT_PER_ALLY` (0.05), then writes `stats.attack = round((_orcBaseAttack + lootAtkBonus) √ó atkMult)` and `stats.defense = round(_orcBaseDefense √ó defMult)`. Pristine baselines stamped on `MINION_PLACED`, `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` (rebaselined post-scale by inferring base from current value √∑ live warband multiplier), and at scene boot for save-load via `_captureOrcBaseline` (subtracts active loot bonus before stamping). New balance constants: `ORC_WARBAND_ATK_PCT_PER_ALLY`, `ORC_WARBAND_DEF_PCT_PER_ALLY`. No SaveSystem changes ‚Äî all new fields (`_orcBaseAttack`, `_orcBaseDefense`, `lootAtkBonus`) are plain numbers that JSON-serialize naturally. |
| golem       | Earth Golem      | **Living Architecture** ‚Äî every placed room (incl. boss + corridor) ‚Üí +5 boss HP / +1 DEF permanent. **Earthquake** ‚Äî 1√ó/day day-phase button; pick a room, advs inside take (rooms placed √ó 2) damage. | 1b.2 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-02) | `BossArchetypeSystem` listens for `ROOM_PLACED`/`ROOM_REMOVED` while archetype is golem; tracks `gameState.boss._golem` (`roomsCounted` / `hpApplied` / `defApplied` / `earthquakeUsesLeft` / `firstUseToastShown`) so a save/load and dynamic place/remove stay balanced and don't double-count. On scene init, backfills any rooms not yet counted (handles old saves cleanly). Earthquake: new `BossArchetypeUI` panel above the action bar shows the EARTHQUAKE button only when archetype = golem and phase = day; click ‚Üí arms; next click on a dungeon tile ‚Üí resolves the room ‚Üí emits `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_TARGET` ‚Üí system applies `(rooms √ó 2)` damage to every adv inside (uses `gameState.dungeon.rooms.length`, no cap). Damage routes through `COMBAT_HIT` and triggers `ADVENTURER_DIED` if HP drops to 0 (so RunHistorySystem / boss XP still fire). UI consumes `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_FIRED` and plays a Game-camera shake (450 ms) + a floating `EARTHQUAKE -N` text over the room center. Daily uses reset on `NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED`. First-use toast fires on construction (UI-side gate via `firstUseToastShown` flag, immune to scene-startup ordering). New balance constants: `GOLEM_HP_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_DEF_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_DMG_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_USES_PER_DAY`. Click-on-button gate prevents the room-pick handler from resolving a phantom room when the player clicks the button itself to disarm. |
| beholder    | Beholder Tyrant  | **Petrify Gaze** ‚Äî BossFightScene only; freezes advs 2s every 6s with eye-beam VFX. **Anti-Magic Aura** ‚Äî 2 random rooms/day disable class abilities for the day (+1 per boss level); purple glow VFX | 1b.3 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-02) | Petrify Gaze: `BossArchetypeSystem` listens to `BOSS_FIGHT_STARTED` and starts a Phaser timer that fires every `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_INTERVAL_MS` (6000) for the duration of the fight. Each fire stamps `adv._petrifiedUntil = now + BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_DURATION_MS` (2000) on every adv inside the boss chamber. `BossSystem._tickFightAdv` early-returns while petrified (freeze in place); `BossSystem._runOneRound`'s attackers filter excludes petrified advs (no boss damage that round). VFX: dedicated `_petrifyFxGraphics` layer draws eye-beams from boss to each target + stone-crackle rings on targets, fading over the 2 s freeze window (prior tweens killed before re-fire). Timer torn down on `BOSS_FIGHT_RESOLVED`; lingering `_petrifiedUntil` cleared so survivors aren't stuck. Anti-Magic Aura: `DAY_PHASE_BEGAN` triggers `_rollAntiMagicRooms` ‚Äî Fisher-Yates picks `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_BASE_ROOMS` (2) + `(bossLevel-1) √ó BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_PER_BOSS_LV` (1) random non-boss rooms, stamps `room._antiMagic=true` and `gameState._antiMagicRoomIds=[‚Ä¶]`. `ClassAbilitySystem.update` reads the daily set and skips the `consider*(adv)` switch when an adv stands inside a marked room (existing buffs still tick out via `_tickActiveBuffs`). VFX: `_antiMagicFx` graphics layer paints a soft purple wash + bright outline on each marked room. `NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED` clears marks + the overlay. Save/load safe ‚Äî both per-room flags and the gameState id list serialize naturally; constructor calls `_renderAntiMagicAura` so a mid-day reload still shows the glow. New balance constants: `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_INTERVAL_MS`, `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_DURATION_MS`, `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_BASE_ROOMS`, `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_PER_BOSS_LV`. |
| lich        | Elder Lich       | **Phylactery** ‚Äî unlocks at boss lvl 3; free Heart item (200 HP, heart-full sprite), 4th life. 15% per-adv hunt roll on entry. Only one heart, no replacement if destroyed; with no normal lives, every party hunts the heart. **Necromancy** ‚Äî kills raise as free Skeletons next dawn (last 1 full day, retain class abilities, dead Clerics heal your minions, no minion-cap). | 1b.4 / 1b.5 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-02) ‚Äî Phylactery (1b.4) + Necromancy (1b.5) both shipped this pass | **Phylactery (1b.4):** new `src/data/items.json` registered in Preload; `BuildMenu` `_itemDefs()` filters by archetype + `unlockLevel` + one-per-run, hidden once placed. Items tab now also re-renders on `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` / `PHYLACTERY_PLACED` / `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` so the heart appears/disappears live. `NightPhase._confirmItemPlacement` validates non-boss room + floor tile, stamps `gameState.phylactery = { instanceId, roomId, tileX, tileY, worldX, worldY, resources: { hp, maxHp }, spriteKey, placedDay }`. New `PhylacteryRenderer` paints `heart-full` sprite + 28px HP bar with hurt-flash; instantiated in `Game.js` and ticked each frame. `BossSystem._endFight` was extended: when `winner='party'` drains `deathsRemaining` to 0 AND `phylactery.resources.hp > 0`, the system bumps `deathsRemaining` back to 1 and refills boss HP, swallowing the final-death event and emitting `PHYLACTERY_REVIVED_BOSS` instead. AISystem: new `HUNT_PHYLACTERY` goal type wired into `_goalToTile` (path target = phyl tile; falls back to FLEE if heart gone) and `_onGoalReached` (freeze adv on arrival; only re-pick when heart destroyed). `BossArchetypeSystem._onAdvsSpawned` rolls `LICH_PHYLACTERY_HUNT_CHANCE` (0.15) per adv on dungeon entry ‚Äî or forces 100% when `boss.deathsRemaining ‚â§ 0`. New `tick(delta)` runs from `Game.update()` real-time: every `LICH_PHYLACTERY_DMG_INTERVAL_MS` (800 ms), advs adjacent to the heart's tile with `HUNT_PHYLACTERY` deal `stats.attack` damage; when HP hits 0 the system fires `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` once, drops `gameState.phylactery`, and routes surviving hunters to FLEE. Unlock toast (`PHYLACTERY_UNLOCKED`) fires on `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` (and on scene boot for save-load) the first time `boss.level ‚â• 3`; gated by `boss._lich.unlockToastShown`. `BossArchetypeUI` consumes that event + `PHYLACTERY_REVIVED_BOSS` + `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` and shows toasts. New balance constants: `LICH_PHYLACTERY_UNLOCK_LEVEL`, `LICH_PHYLACTERY_HUNT_CHANCE`, `LICH_PHYLACTERY_DMG_INTERVAL_MS`. **Necromancy (1b.5):** `_onAdvDied` queues `{ classId, name, level, tileX, tileY }` onto `gameState._lich.pendingRaises` whenever the active boss is the lich. `_onDayBegan` (DAY_PHASE_BEGAN listener) culls expired raised first via `_cullExpiredRaised` (cull rule: `today < m._expireAtDay`), then drains the pending queue via `_raiseQueuedDead`: spawns `skeleton1` via `createMinion` at the boss-chamber center (offset around a small ring so they don't stack), with `class: 'garrison'` (so they don't count toward the roster cap), `isUndead: true` (so MinionAISystem.respawnAll permanently removes them on death), `_raisedFromAdvDeath: true`, `_raisedClassId`, `_raisedAdvName`, `_expireAtDay = today + NECROMANCY_LIFESPAN_DAYS` (1, so they vanish at the very next dawn). `_applyClassRetentionBuffs` adjusts base stats per the dead adv's class (cleric: +DEF, range 2, support tag; mage: +ATK, range 3, arcane damage; ranger: +ATK, range 3; knight: +HP +DEF; barbarian: +ATK -DEF; monk: +SPD; rogue: +ATK +SPD; others: +1 ATK). Boss-level scaling re-applied on top via `applyBossLevelToMinion`. Raised cleric heal: `_tickRaisedClerics` runs each frame from `tick(delta)`, every `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_INTERVAL_MS` (2200) heals the most-wounded ally minion within Manhattan dist 3 for `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_AMOUNT` (4). Events: `NECROMANCY_RAISED { count, minionIds }`, `NECROMANCY_RAISED_EXPIRED { count }`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL { sourceId, targetId, amount }`. New balance constants: `NECROMANCY_LIFESPAN_DAYS`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_AMOUNT`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_INTERVAL_MS`. |

On entering a fresh door tile it stores the cp on `m._doorPatLastCp` and snapshots `m._doorPatLockedSnapshot = !!cp.locked`, then calls `DungeonRenderer.openDoor(cp)` so the door visibly swings open during traversal. On stepping off the door tile it calls `DungeonRenderer.closeDoor(cp)` (which now mirrors to the paired cp on its own ‚Äî matching `openDoor`'s behavior) and restores `cp.locked = true` if the snapshot recorded it. Behavior is generic ‚Äî automatically benefits Vampire Thralls, Demon Imps, and Wraith Haunt Ghosts. Tracking state self-cleans on death/no-tag. |

## 2. Personalities (target: 18 from design ‚Äî **17 active** after 3 removals; reconciled 2026-05-31)

> Reconciled 2026-05-31: `personalities.json` holds **17** ids (greedy, paranoid, speed_runner, completionist, martyr, coward, overconfident, cartographer, solo, raid_leader, underdog, inquisitor, vulture, traumatized, the_fan, echo, mimic_handler). The original target was 18; party_loyal, vandal, and beast_tamer were removed (rows below), and echo + mimic_handler were added post-design. (Inquisitor since removed 2026-06-09 ‚Üí 16 live.) **Note:** personality data still carries dead fields (`decisionOverrides`, `reactions`, unused tags).
>
> ‚öÝ **SUPERSEDED BY the AI & Personality Overhaul (2026-06-10).** The deferred "full personality
> revamp" is now spec'd ‚Äî see DESIGN.md ‚Üí "Adventurer AI & Personality Overhaul" + the
> "AI & Personality Overhaul" ledger lower in THIS file. That spec cuts speed_runner/the_fan/
> mimic_handler, reworks coward+underdog, builds martyr+raid_leader for real, adds 5 new
> personalities, flattens the roll (equal/ungated), and gives every personality real verbs via the
> nerve/appraisal/social substrate. The rows below are the pre-overhaul state.

> 24 damned**. The "64 pacts (2026-05-02)" note below is the historical snapshot at that batch;
> the pool grew via ¬ß5a (24 damned) + ¬ß5b (8 new legendaries) + later additions. Use 96 as the
> current count.

Marionette possession: click-to-possess + WASD + auto-attack + camera follow + MinionAISystem suppression of other dungeon minions while possessed; releases on minion death / NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED / DAY_PHASE_STARTED.) **63 pacts** ‚Äî Phase 9 Batches A‚ÄìH all shipped today. Original 13 (taxation_of_souls, bloodbound, gold_rush, undying_horde, sealed_paths, pack_synergy, blood_money, hasty_architect, great_erasure, schism, glory_hounds, sworn_rivals, famine_decree) + 50 new (Batch A: gilded_demise, pyramid_scheme, ransom_note, tax_the_living, tower_tax, crusaders_curse; Batch B: kennel_discipline, ironhide_rite, frenzy_pact, last_stand_doctrine, mage_hunt, vampires_toll; Batch C: tyrants_gaze, soul_tether, avengers_rite, final_breath; Batch D: false_maps, whispered_lies, open_book, whisperers_tongue; Batch E: doomsday_clock, the_long_game, inquisitors_mark; Batch F: summon_adds_i/ii/iii, drill_sergeant, endless_garrison, the_cull, trap_masons_touch, trapsmiths_guild, forbidden_workshop, architects_vision; Batch G: hellfire_breath, lightning_strike, shockwave_slam, spectral_reach, dark_vortex, soul_drain, doppelgangers, petrifying_stare; Batch H: cursed_soil, sundered_floor, pact_of_the_mirror, pact_of_the_cartographer, pact_of_the_jester, pact_of_the_whisperer, pact_of_the_brand, pact_of_the_reaper, pact_of_the_crucible). ### 5a. Damned Pacts ‚Äî solid-black tier (2026-05-28 ‚Äî ‚úÖ all 24 implemented + headless-tested; 3 flow/UI ones flagged for playtest)

New **6th rarity tier** (`damned`, rendered solid black). Devil's-bargain pacts: `description` = the small one-time bribe (the green "Deal", paid in `onActivate`), `tradeoffDescription` = the huge permanent curse (the red "Price"). Schema is NOT inverted ‚Äî that mapping renders correctly in the existing Deal/Price UI. **Delivery:** 10% chance the Dark Pact grimoire is black ‚Üí offers an all-Damned hand; otherwise Damned pacts mix into the normal pool at Epic draw weight (the tier just before Legendary ‚Äî weight 10). Permanent + unlimited stacking like normal pacts. Schema reuse ‚Äî no new fields. Gold-lump bribes are flat (values provisional, see DESIGN.md). Full spec lives in DESIGN.md ¬ß "Damned Pacts". Tier wiring touches `PactCard.js` / `PactPicker.js` (add `damned` to RARITY maps + RARITY_GLYPH), `DungeonMechanicSystem._weightedSample` / `TIER_WEIGHTS` + `getOfferings`, and the DarkPact popup (`DarkPactPopup.js` / `PactPicker.js`) for the black-grimoire roll.

### 5b. Legendary expansion (2026-05-28 ‚Äî ‚úÖ 8 new, pool 8‚Üí16 legendaries; headless-verified 25/25)

Normal-schema legendaries (massive upside/downside). Boss-stat boons flow through `BossSystem._recomputeBossFightStats` (per-stat multipliers, verified via real recompute). Boss-fight-internal effects (invincibility window, HP-scaled attack, 5√ó damage) verified at flag + code-inspection level ‚Äî **want a live boss-fight playtest**.

| ID | Name | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| colossus_heart | Colossus Heart | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | HP x2 + atk x0.5 via recompute boon (verified 400/6). BOSS_STATS_DIRTY forces refresh |
| the_apex_tyrant | The Apex Tyrant | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | HP x2/atk x1.5/def x1.5 (recompute, verified 400/18/15); waves x2 permanent (DayPhase apexTyrant) |
| avatar_of_ruin | Avatar of Ruin | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | maxHP x0.5 (recompute, verified 100); invincible first **5s** (_applyDamageToBoss + _fightStartedAt). **Playtest** |
| wrath_unbound | Wrath Unbound | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | up to +100% atk as HP falls + +50% dmg taken. Now via `_bossAtkScaled` on ALL boss-damage sites (melee/slam/abilities), verified √ó1.5@50%/√ó2@0. |
| crown_of_avarice | Crown of Avarice | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | gold x2 (AISystem goldMul + treasury); every 5th day hero raid (DayPhase wave x2 + +50% adv stats). Verified cadence+buff |
| the_iron_price | The Iron Price | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | minions x2 (CombatSystem) + traps x2 (trapDamageMult); gold income zeroed (AISystem goldMul=0 + treasury x0) |
| sudden_death | Sudden Death | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | everyone x5: CombatSystem (minion<->adv) + trapDamageMult + boss fight (_applyDamageToBoss intake + `_bossAtkScaled` on ALL boss-damage sites). |
| the_undying_court | The Undying Court | LG | ‚úÖ DONE | Class-accurate raise (mirrors Lich): skeleton1 base + `_raisedClassId`/`_raisedSpriteVariant` (renders as the dead adv) + carried stats + `bossArchetypeSystem._applyClassRetentionBuffs` for the kit. Full slots sacrifice 2; living advs +2%/member. Verified. |

## 6. Dungeon room types

**Note (2026-04-30):** The original 9-room design list and the Phase-2/QW additions were **superseded by the Room redesign 2026-04-30** in DESIGN.md. The new spec defines 21 rooms organized around gateway/cap/scaling rules. Existing handler code for removed rooms remains in place as orphaned no-ops; cleanup is a follow-up phase.

### 6a. Required / Fixed

| ID | Name | Cap | Unlock | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| boss_chamber | Boss Chamber | 1 (fixed) | Start | 2 | ‚úÖ DONE | fixed centerpiece, kept |
| entry_hall | Entry Hall | 1 / 2 / 3 (forced) | Start; L5; L10 | 3 | ‚úÖ DONE | required entrance; multi-entry (2026-05-20) ‚Äî random per-adventurer spawn entry + flee-to-nearest, 2nd Entry Hall forced @ boss L5, 3rd @ L10 |

### 6b. Starter (free, L1)

| ID | Name | Cap | Unlock | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| starter_corridor | Corridor | scales 2‚Üí20 (+2/level) | L1, free | 2 | ‚è≥ PENDING (audit 2026-05-22) | Room exists, no behaviour. Cap-scaling-by-level still not implemented. |
| starter_barracks | Barracks | scales 1‚Üí5 | L1, free | 2 | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | ‚úÖ +10 roster slots per Barracks wired (`NightPhase.js` ~line 1714); ‚úÖ sneakable behaviour data present; ‚úÖ roster-vs-garrison minion split shipped (`Minion.js` `class` field defaults to `'roster'`, NightPhase enforces cap, garrison minions exempt). **Remaining**: per-Barracks 1‚Üí5 cap-scaling-by-level. |
| starter_guard_post | Guard Post | unlimited | L1 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `MinionAISystem._pickTarget` adds a Guard-Post forward-operating-base check (`isGuardPost`) ‚Äî minions whose home room is a starter_guard_post engage adventurers in any room directly door-connected to the post, bypassing the same-room requirement but NOT escalating to whole-dungeon hunt. Existing `_walkAlongPath` handles cross-door travel; existing no-target return-home flow brings them back when the connected rooms clear. Garrison minions still hard-bound. |

### 6c. New rooms ‚Äî Room redesign 2026-04-30

| ID | Name | Cap | Unlock | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| crypt | Crypt | 3 | L2 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `RoomBehaviorSystem._onNightStart` spawns 4 garrison Risen Bones per Crypt, refilled nightly, room-bound (`class: 'garrison'`, `assignedRoomId` pinned). |
| trap_factory | Trap Factory | scales 1‚Üí5 | L3 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Each Factory adds `f.trapSlotsPerFactory ?? 5` to the global trap-slot cap (`NightPhase.js` ~line 1883, surfaced in LeftPanels). No upgrade tree per design. |
| treasury | Treasury | scales 1‚Üí5 | L3 | TBD | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | ‚úÖ Daily flat 5-gold stipend per Treasury (`RoomBehaviorSystem.js` line 60-64) ‚Äî replaces the original 4-chest model after the 2026-05-02 loot-pickup retirement. **Remaining (or DEVIATION_NOTED?)**: original design had "4 chests + alive-exit-required theft + raises adventurer arrival rate"; both the chest model and the arrival-rate raise are not implemented. User to confirm whether to keep stipend-only or re-design. |
| armory | Armory | scales 1‚Üí3 | L3 | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | ‚úÖ Adjacency +2 ATK buff for minions in rooms door-connected to an active Armory (`CombatSystem.js` ~line 567). **Remaining**: 1‚Üí3 cap-scaling-by-level. |
| library_of_whispers | Library of Whispers | 1 | L2 | TBD | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | ‚úÖ Tier-1 forecast: next day's party size + class composition computed nightly into `meta.nextPartyPreview` + `LIBRARY_FORECAST` event (`RoomBehaviorSystem.js` ~line 70). **Remaining**: L6 +personalities / L8 +stats/equipment / L10 +planned route tier scaling. |
| watchtower | Watchtower | 2 | L5 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | First-strike aura: minions in any room door-connected to an active Watchtower get one free hit on adv entry, bypassing range + cooldown, runs through `CombatSystem._computeDamage` so armory/marked modifiers still apply (`RoomBehaviorSystem._fireWatchtowerStrike`). |
| wandering_gate | Wandering Gate | 1 | L6 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | 60% neighbour / 35% any built room / 5% Boss Chamber teleport on entry, per-day cooldown (`RoomBehaviorSystem._teleportFromWanderingGate`). |
| veil_of_forgetting | Veil of Forgetting | 1 | L6 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Each NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED, scrubs `knowledge.sharedPool` entries (rooms / enemiesPerRoom / traps / loot) for every room door-connected to each Veil, excluding boss_chamber + entry_hall. Emits `VEIL_ERASED_INTEL`. |
| catacombs | Catacombs | 2 | L7 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Death-in-room ‚Üí spawn Tier-2 Revenant garrison via `AISystem._kill` (~line 3097). |
| mimic_vault | Mimic Vault | 1 | L7 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî REWORKED 2026-05-22 | Disguised as Treasury; 2 chest-disguised mimics per day (state: 'chest'). Each mimic rolls a `chestTier` (1..10) at spawn ‚Äî MinionRenderer paints them as the matching `item-treasure-chest-<tier>` sprite with a red tint (`0xff5050`) for player visibility; adv AI ignores the tint. KnowledgeSystem.observeRoomContents adds disguised mimics to `adv.knowledge.treasureChests` with an `_isMimic` flag so the standard chest-tempt loop picks them up. `AISystem._tryTriggerMimic` (runs alongside `_tryOpenTreasureChest` on every tile step) springs an unknowing adv within 1 tile: `mimicState‚Üí'sprung'`, MIMIC_SPRUNG emitted, all alive advs + sharedPool gain `knowledge.mimics[id]`, opener killed via `_kill`. `_resetSprungMimics` flips state back to 'chest' on NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED. Knowledge-aware advs see through the disguise (allow-list in MinionAISystem `_pickTarget` adv-side filter); MinionAISystem retaliation carve-out lets mimics swing back when attacked. The placeable Mimic minion (Barracks roster) uses the exact same path. *(Reworked from the original 40%/5% open-roll + 30% max-HP bite + reveal-and-engage mechanic ‚Äî replaced with stationary instant-kill trap per user 2026-05-22.)* |
| hall_of_trials | Hall of Trials | scales 1‚Üí3 | L7 | TBD | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | ‚úÖ Nightly spawn of random T2 evolved minion (garrison) per Hall, if none alive (`RoomBehaviorSystem.js` ~line 219). **Remaining**: 1‚Üí3 cap-scaling-by-level. |
| wishing_well | Wishing Well | 1 | L8 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Coin flip on first entry per day. Heads: +3 ATK, +20 maxHp, full heal. Tails: `flags.marked` = +50% damage from minions until end of day (`RoomBehaviorSystem._rollWishingWell`). |
| false_exit | False Exit | 1 | L8 | QW | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Fleeing adventurers entering a False Exit are teleported adjacent to the boss chamber and forced into AT_BOSS goal + fighting state ‚Äî they thought they were leaving, the dungeon kept them (`RoomBehaviorSystem._teleportToNearBoss`). |
| hall_of_madness | Hall of Madness | 1 | L9 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Friendly-fire AI state: while in a Hall of Madness, an adventurer rolls each tick to attack a same-party ally (`AISystem.js` ~line 2161), saves their previous goal, and restores it on leaving the room. New `ATTACK_ALLY` goal type. |
| throne_room | Throne Room | scales 1‚Üí2 | L9 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî DEVIATION (audit 2026-05-22) | 1 Mini-Boss per Throne Room nightly, garrison/room-bound, stats scaled by current boss level via `MINION_HP_PER_BOSS_LV` + `MINION_ATK_PER_BOSS_LV` (`RoomBehaviorSystem.js` ~line 246). DEVIATION: original "T1‚ÜíT2‚ÜíT3 family progression" simplified to a fixed skeleton3 baseline whose stats scale instead. Visual family-swap is deferred polish; mechanic intent (escalating threat) is preserved via stat scaling. Noted in DESIGN.md 2026-05-22. |
| sanctum | Sanctum | 1 | L10 (capstone) | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Boss HP regen between fights: +8 HP per Sanctum per round (`BossSystem.js` ~line 1835). Minion regen aura: minions in any room door-connected to an active Sanctum get the barracks-style regen treatment (`MinionAISystem._isAdjacentToSanctum`). |

### 6d. Top-level rules (Room redesign 2026-04-30)

| Rule | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| Roster vs Garrison minion split | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `Minion.js` carries `class: 'roster' \| 'garrison'` (default `'roster'`). `NightPhase._rosterUsed/_rosterCap` enforces +10-per-Barracks cap; garrison minions (Crypt, Mimic Vault, Hall of Trials, Throne Room, Catacombs revenants) are excluded from the cap and AI-pinned to their `assignedRoomId`. |
| "Adjacent / connected" = direct shared door | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `dungeonGrid.getNeighborRooms(instanceId)` returns rooms that share a connection-point, not transitive ‚Äî consumed by Veil, Sanctum, Watchtower, Wandering Gate. |
| Alive-exit-required for chest/loot theft | TBD | üö´ SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Original 4-chest Treasury + loot-pickup-on-escape model was retired 2026-05-02 in the loot-pickup cleanup. Treasury became a flat daily stipend; Mimic Vault became a chest-disguise-and-bite mechanic. The "alive-exit-required" rule is no longer relevant to the current design. |
| Cap scaling by boss level | TBD | üü° PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | Some scaling exists (throne-room mini-boss stats, library forecast size, beacon buff bonus). The unified per-room cap-scaling-by-level table from DESIGN.md is **not** implemented ‚Äî caps are mostly fixed-per-instance with +X-per-Room aggregation. |
| Boss level cap = 10 | TBD | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Boss level capped at 10 in current BossSystem. |

## 7. Trap types

**2026-05-20 redesign.** The original 3 standard + 9 interaction traps were scrapped ‚Äî none ever shipped (`trapTypes.json` was always `[]`; the old `TrapSystem`/`Trap`/`TrapRenderer` code targeted that dead roster). Replaced by the 8-trap roster below. Old rows preserved in git history.

### 7a. Current roster (8 traps) ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE

| ID | Name | Footprint | Placement | Trigger | Unlock | Gold | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| spike_pillar | Spike Pillar | 2√ó2 | floor | adv within 1 tile | L3 | 20 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| shooting_arrows | Shooting Arrows | 1 wall tile | wall (not doorway) | adv in LOS lane | L4 | 30 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| rotating_blades | Rotating Blades | 2√ó2 | floor | adv in adjacent tile | L4 | 25 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| bomb | Bomb | 1√ó1 | floor | adv within 2 tiles ‚Üí 3s fuse | L5 | 35 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| saw_blade | Saw Blade | 3-tile track | floor | saw overlaps adv | L6 | 35 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| spike_pit | Spike Pit | 2√ó2 | floor (fully interior) | stepped on | L6 | 40 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| cannon | Cannon | 1√ó1 | floor | adv in LOS (faced dir) | L7 | 45 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| dragon_trap | Dragon Trap | 1 wall tile | wall (not doorway) | adv in LOS lane | L8 | 55 | ‚úÖ DONE |

Locked specs: 1 Trap-Factory slot each; never in boss room / entry hall. Trap Factory (gateway room) unlocks at boss L3; traps unlock L3‚Äì8. Trap damage scales +12%/boss level (`Balance.TRAP_DAMAGE_PER_BOSS_LV`); trap gold cost scales +20%/boss level (`Balance.TRAP_COST_PER_BOSS_LV`) ‚Äî both mirror the minion system. Gold values in `trapTypes.json` are the level-1 base. Knowledge gained only on trigger or damage-survived. Area/contact hazards hit both factions; LOS projectile traps hit adventurers only and are confined to the trap's own room (lane stops at walls/doors).

### 7b. Cross-cutting infrastructure (new ‚Äî none of this existed) ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE

| Item | Phase | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Multi-tile (2√ó2) footprint + placement validation | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Wall-mounted placement category + auto-door suppression | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Trap collision (solid-tile registration for pathfinding) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Line-of-sight scan (room-confined; canned projectile animations) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Proximity / radius / adjacent-contact triggers | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Continuous-damage zones (blades / saw / pillar) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Moving trap (saw track travel ‚Äî time-based wave) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Trap rotation + R-key handling (cannon only) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Poison damage-over-time status effect | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Bomb fuse countdown + 5-tile-radius explosion + chain | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Knowledge gain (trigger / damage-survived) ‚Üí pathfinder routing | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Trap damage scales with boss level (+12%/lvl) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Rewrite `Trap.js` / `TrapSystem.js` / `TrapRenderer.js` (old roster) | TRAPS | ‚úÖ DONE |

> have confirmed dedicated `_tickXxx` handlers in `MinionAISystem.js`. **scavenger, engineer,
> mourner, echo** were reported as missing or only partially wired despite the ‚úÖ below ‚Äî
> re-verify each against the code before trusting its status. Also note **mimic_handler is a
> *personality*** (¬ß2 / `personalities.json`), not a minion behavior type ‚Äî the row below
> mislabels it. None of these 9 are actual minion *types* in `minionTypes.json`; they're
> behavior/role tags. Don't trust this sub-section's ‚úÖ marks without a grep.

| engineer | Engineer | 6e | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî passive 1.25√ó damage buff on traps in same room |

| mimic_handler | Mimic Handler | QW | ‚úÖ DONE | personalities.json + AISystem._pickNextGoal filters out item.isMimicSpawn loot for mimic_handler-tagged advs |
| whisperer | Whisperer | QW | ‚úÖ DONE | MinionAISystem._tickWhisperer corrupts a random sharedKnowledge entry every 10s ‚Äî accuracy capped at 0.3, trap tile coords jittered ¬±2 |

| echo | Echo | QW | ‚úÖ DONE | MinionAISystem stamps minion.mimickedClassId from the last-seen adventurer; CombatSystem._computeDamage uses it for class-flavored damage (mage spells, cleric smite, ranger arrows, rogue backstab) |

> `evolutionPaths` field (which is empty by design). An earlier audit pass mistook the empty
> field for "evolutions broken" ‚Äî that was a false alarm. The named rows below should be
> cross-checked against `minionEvolutions.json` ids, but the mechanism is live.

|---|---|---|---|
| Plague Bringer | killMethod: poison, 3 kills | 7 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî data + EvolutionSystem condition matcher |

| Bone Crusher | killedClassType: knight, 5 kills | 7 | ‚úÖ DONE |

## 11. Knowledge system

| Item | Phase | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Per-adventurer knowledge of rooms / minions / traps | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî `adv.knowledge.{rooms,traps,minions}` populated by KnowledgeSystem |
| Knowledge accumulates as adventurer enters dungeon | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî `observeCurrentRoom` per tick + `observeMinion` on engagement scan |
| Knowledge sharing on flee (to other adventurers) | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî merges into `gameState.sharedKnowledge` with personality-specific accuracy |
| Knowledge accuracy flag (some intel is wrong) | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî accuracy multiplier, `'rumor'` source, partial accurate flag |
| Adventurer returns leading party with prior knowledge | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî *was silently dead until 2026-05-20:* `rollReturnLeader()` was never implemented, so the DayPhase returning-leader block never ran (every wave inherited at the partial rate, never the full-briefing 1.0). `rollReturnLeader()` now exists ‚Äî KNOWLEDGE_RETURN_CHANCE gates a recently-fled survivor (within KNOWLEDGE_RETURN_MAX_AGE_DAYS) returning as the wave leader |
| Knowledge affects pathfinding cost | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî PathfinderSystem accepts `costFn`; trap-known tiles get 6√ó multiplier |
| Veteran return notification | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-20) ‚Äî returning leader carries `escapeCount` ‚Üí ToastQueue "VETERAN APPROACHING" toast on entry; also emits `VETERAN_APPROACHING` for the Dungeon Log |
| Veterans stronger than normal adventurers | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-20) ‚Äî boss-level scaled like any adventurer, then √ó`KNOWLEDGE_VETERAN_HP_MULT` (1.2) / √ó`KNOWLEDGE_VETERAN_ATK_MULT` (1.15) |
| Veterans worth double gold | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-20) ‚Äî `goldMul √ó2` for `returningVeteran` in the AISystem kill-reward chain |
| Veterans visually distinct at a glance | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-20) ‚Äî gold aura ring + body stroke + "‚òÖ VET n" badge in AdventurerRenderer |
| Returning veteran identity continuity | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-05-20) ‚Äî returning leader reuses the survivor's `instanceId` so re-flees accumulate `runCount`; `KnowledgeSystem._onAdventurerDied` purges a veteran killed in the dungeon (their championed intel leaves the shared pool) |

## 16. Adventurer behavior decisions

| Item | Phase | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Goal: SEEK_BOSS | 4 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Goal: EXPLORE_ROOM | 5 | ‚úÖ DONE |
| Goal: SEEK_LOOT | 7b | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî fires when adventurer's lootPriority > 0.6 and floor loot exists; pickups transfer to adv.gear |
| Goal: FLEE (leave dungeon) | 6 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî triggered by hp < personality.fleeThreshold |
| Goal: SLEEP (heal in dungeon) | 6e | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî sleeps when HP < 0.4 + no potions + no hostiles, regens 3 HP/sec |
| Goal: HEAL (use potion / cleric) | 6c | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî adventurers sip potions at HP < 0.4 if any in inventory; cleric heals allies in range |
| Goal: FOLLOW_PARTY | 10 | ‚úÖ DONE | echo personality uses FOLLOW_LEADER goal targeting party-leader's tile (functionally identical) |
| Goal: AVOID_ENEMY (knowledge-driven) | 8 | ‚úÖ DONE | KnowledgeSystem.costMultiplierForTile already applies KNOWLEDGE_TRAP_COST_MULTIPLIER (6√ó) on tiles with known traps ‚Äî pathfinder routes around them |
| Goal: SCOUT | 5/8 | ‚úÖ DONE | cartographer-tagged advs prioritise EXPLORE_ROOM goals via personality lootPriority/explorationDrive weights |
| Decision to fight / leave / sleep based on stats | 6/6c/6e | ‚úÖ DONE | AISystem cowardShouldFlee (HP < threshold), resourceExhaustedShouldFlee (mage/ranger), shouldSleep (HP < POTION_HEAL_THRESHOLD) all live |
| Returning next day with knowledge + better gear | 8b | ‚úÖ DONE | KnowledgeSystem.rollReturnLeader + DayPhase priorPathHistory hand-off + RETURNING_GEAR_BONUS_HP/ATK |

## 21. Minion meta

> **üîÑ PROGRESSION OVERHAUL ‚Äî 2026-05-29.** The kill-driven minion progression was replaced with a gold-gated one (user-directed):
> - **Minion kill-XP / per-minion levels REMOVED.** `EvolutionSystem` no longer awards minion XP or applies level stats (adventurer XP in Phase 7b is untouched).
> - **Auto kill-evolution REMOVED.** Minions no longer mutate up their chain after 2 kills. `MinionEvolutionSystem` now exposes `upgrade(minion)` ‚Äî a **player-paid, gold-gated tier advance** (night-phase UPGRADE tool, left of SELL). Cost = chain-root build cost √ó `MINION_UPGRADE_TIER_MULT[tier]` √ó `buildScaleMul` (escalates per tier + scales with the run).
> - **Upgrades PERSIST through death.** `upgrade()` re-bases `_baseMaxHp`/`_baseAtk` to the new tier, so a revived minion returns at its paid tier (no chain[0] reset; `applyResets` removed).
> - **Day-scaling REMOVED.** Minions scale by **boss level only** (`MINION_*_PER_DAY = 0`); their displayed LV = boss level.
> - **`evolutionPaths` kept as flavour only** ‚Äî name + ability, stat deltas stripped (no raw power).

| Item | Phase | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Minion naming | 7 ‚Üí reworked 2026-05-29 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî names now come from `evolutionPath` specializations (kill-themed rename + ability) instead of the removed level-up auto-name; players can also rename manually |
| Player can rename minions | QW | ‚úÖ DONE | MinionInspector ‚úé icon next to name opens window.prompt; sets minion.name + emits MINION_NAMED |
| Gold-gated tier upgrades | ‚Äî 2026-05-29 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî UPGRADE tool ‚Üí confirm popup (before‚Üíafter preview) ‚Üí `MinionEvolutionSystem.upgrade`; colour-coded glow ring marks upgradeable minions; TIER badge above sprite + in roster/inspector |
| Bounty status flag | 7 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî `minion.hasBounty` set at BOUNTY_KILL_THRESHOLD kills |
| Per-minion kill history | 6 | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî populated by CombatSystem on kill events |

Tier-first weighted draw via TIER_WEIGHTS in _weightedSample (45/25/15/10/5). DarkPactPopup shows rarity tags with shine animations on rare/epic/legendary. | ‚úÖ DONE |
| 9b ‚Äî Dungeon polish | Dossier UI, trap memory UI, paranoia chest indicators, auto-pause on key events, inquisitor mechanic disable, adventurers fight over loot, spectral ghost spawning | ‚úÖ DONE (Hidden keys + locked doors, mimic AI, echo personality moved to Phase 10) |
| 10 ‚Äî Boss Fight + Polish (kernel) | BossSystem with auto-resolved fight, BossFightOverlay, GameOver eulogy, Graveyard scene, ReputationSystem + tier ladder + legendary spawns, Mimic minion + Mimicry Plague reveals, Echo personality, key/locked-door foundation | ‚úÖ DONE |
| 10b ‚Äî Endgame polish | Boss evolution tree (6 nodes), Summon Adds ability, lava_floor + collapsing_pillars hazards, guild raid teams at feared+ reputation, endless mode continue, hardcore/no-traps/all-raids challenge runs, 5 new boss archetypes, Graveyard sort/filter, twitch_streamer chat_poll | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî Supabase leaderboard + 5 more archetypes + locked-door pathfinder block remain explicit defers |

## 30. Sprite-based dungeon tiling ‚Äî themes + tileset editor + room template editor

> See DESIGN.md ‚Üí "Sprite-based dungeon tiling" for the full spec.
> Three-phase build (A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C). Each row "data + UI + persistence + game wiring".

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| theme-schema | Theme JSON schema (slots: floor, 10 wall slots, 24 door slots; per-slot variant arrays) | 30A | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî DEVIATION (audit 2026-05-22) | `assets/themes/manifest.json` lists 40+ tile sprites (walls, pillars, doors, corners, floors 1-31, dirt floors, wall holes) loaded via `Preload`. Per-room theme indirection skipped ‚Äî see `theme-per-room` row. |
| sprite-library | Sprite library (PNGs + per-sprite metadata: srcSize 32/64/128, mode scale\|span, tags) | 30A | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `assets/themes/sprites/*.png` + `assets/themes/manifest.json`; loaded as `themesprite-<id>` texture keys in `Preload.js`. |
| variant-pick | Random pick per cell at dungeon-build time, persisted in dungeon state (no per-frame flicker) | 30A | üö´ SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Replaced by explicit per-cell authoring: every room's `tileLayout` in `rooms.json` names the exact sprite per cell. No runtime random variant pick needed. |
| fs-handle | File System Access API wrapper (pick project root once, persist handle in IndexedDB, write PNGs + JSON) | 30A | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Used by `RoomTileEditor.js` to write changes back to disk. |
| tileset-editor | Tile-theme authoring: upload tiles under a theme (auto-slot by filename), slot-coverage grid, live preview, full-room PNG skins | 30A | ‚úÖ DONE ‚Äî folded into Room Editor (2026-06-05) | Standalone `TilesetEditor.js` RETIRED + deleted; theme/tile/skin authoring now lives in `RoomTileEditor.js`'s ‚öô Themes + üé® Skins modals. |
| theme-per-room | Each room template in rooms.json gets a `theme: "<name>"` field | 30A | üö´ SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Per-room `theme:` indirection abandoned in favour of direct per-cell `tileLayout` authoring on each room. 0/21 rooms currently carry a `theme` field. |
| room-tile-editor | RoomTileEditor scene: load any room template, paint cells with library sprites, save tileLayout back to rooms.json | 30B | ‚úÖ DONE | uses existing `tileLayout` field on rooms.json |
| room-tile-rotation | Per-cell rotation in RoomTileEditor: R-key / UI button cycles brush 0/90/180/270; cell entries become `string \| { id, rot }`; renderer applies setAngle | 30B+ | ‚úÖ DONE | scope (1) only ‚Äî per-variant rotation in TilesetEditor not yet planned |
| room-tile-mirror | Per-cell horizontal + vertical mirror toggles on the brush. Cell entries gain optional `flipH`, `flipV` booleans; renderer applies image.flipX / flipY. Composes with rotation. | 30B+ | ‚è≥ PENDING | brush state persists across MainMenu round-trips like rotation does |
| renderer-sprite-path | DungeonRenderer adds sprite-based tile path; consumes active theme + per-cell overrides; falls back to procedural when no theme | 30C | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `DungeonRenderer` paints rooms from their `tileLayout` (string \| `{id, rot}` per cell) using `themesprite-<id>` textures and the `_themeTextureKey()` helper. Falls back to procedural when no layout. |
| span-rendering | Renderer honors span sprites: 64 covers 2√ó2 anchor, 128 covers 4√ó4; covered cells skipped | 30C | ‚è≥ PENDING | Not yet implemented ‚Äî current per-cell pipeline assumes 32px tiles only. Low priority unless larger sprites land. |
| mainmenu-runes | MainMenu gets TILESET EDITOR + ROOM EDITOR runes | 30A/B | ‚úÖ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Both runes present in `MainMenuOverlay`, gated behind the `'mango'` cheat name. |

| event-cursed-relic | Cursed Relic ‚Äî night modal CLAIM/BANISH; CLAIM drops a cursed Tier-5 chest (gold/day) that DOUBLES every wave (with a daily toast) until sold | EV | ‚úÖ DONE | minBossLevel 1. | event-saboteur | The Saboteur ‚Äî lone invulnerable all-black ninja-rogue replaces the wave; tours every trap disabling it (re-arms overnight), then flees | EV | ‚úÖ DONE | minBossLevel 2. New `DISARM_TRAP` goal; minions ignore `_saboteur`; traps can't damage `_invulnerable`. Dark-tinted rogue sprite. |
| event-treasure-raid | **Treasure Hunters (2026-05-29; üîÑ scheduling reverted 2026-06-01)** ‚Äî a **normal shuffle-bag dungeon event**. It was briefly a dedicated **10-day "Treasure Raid" track** (days 10/20/30‚Ä¶, pulled out of the shuffle bag); **that track was removed 2026-06-01 by user request** ‚Äî it now rolls randomly in the regular rotation again, gated only on a non-empty treasury (`_eventPrecondMet` ‚Üí `player.gold > 0`). The day's **normal-size wave + active modifiers** all arrive as treasure hunters. Raiders steal **liquid gold** (choice B): each escapee carries off a share of `0.80 √ó day-start treasury √∑ party-size`, **capped at 80% loss / 20% floor**; killed raiders steal nothing (whole wave escapes = 80%, half = ~40%, all killed = 0). Collision: raid **preempts** a regular event due that day. Chest-rush is now pure visual flavor (chest income is `opened`-independent + resets nightly). | EV | ‚úÖ DONE | EventSystem: the `nextRaidDay`/`scheduledIsRaid` 10-day track was removed 2026-06-01 ‚Äî `treasure_hunters` now flows through the normal `_eligibleEvents` shuffle bag (`_eventPrecondMet` gates on `player.gold > 0`). `_skimTreasureRaider` in `_onAdventurerFled` (mirrors the loot-goblin skim, `treasureRaidStartGold`/`StolenToday`/`PartySize` accumulators). DayPhase stamps `treasureRaidPartySize` as it tags `_treasureHunter`. AISystem `_tryOpenTreasureChest` skips the per-chest gold debit for raiders (+`_raiderLooted` latch ‚Üí ESCAPE_WITH_LOOT). Night chest-sell-block + announce banner reuse the existing `scheduledId==='treasure_hunters'` paths. 10-day interval + 80% cap are the tunable knobs. |

---

## 34. UI / HUD overhaul v2 ‚Äî claude-design DOM port (2026-05-18)

> Second pass on the HUD chrome. Section 31's Phaser-rendered Crypt-themed implementation ships and stays default until each panel here lands. Source design files: `D:\Documents\Game Jam Code\Quest-Failed assets\claude design ui\design_handoff_quest_failed_ui\` (high-fidelity HTML/React/CSS mockups; the README in that folder is the source of truth for tokens, animations, and panel layout). Render strategy: DOM overlay on top of the Phaser canvas, vanilla JS modules in `src/hud/`, no build step. A 1920√ó1080 logical stage is transform-scaled to fit the viewport so design coordinates stay literal. Gated behind a feature flag (`?newhud=1` URL param or `localStorage.newhud='1'`) until every Phase 34B panel has shipped ‚Äî then the flag flips default-on and section 31 chrome moves to removed-not-deleted.

## 35. Companion NPC ‚Äî Lilith (2026-05-21)

> **Reconciled 2026-05-31 ‚Äî full roster is 9, not 4.** Sections 35‚Äì40 document the first four
> keepers (Lilith, Malakor, Zul'Gath, Safira) as if they were the complete roster, but
> `companions.js` `COMPANION_ORDER` now has **9**: lilith, safira, rattlebones, necroknight,
> nocturna, malakor, spectra, luna, zulgath. Starters = lilith/malakor/safira; the other 6
> unlock via achievements (rattlebones‚Üêcurtain_call, necroknight‚Üêmonarch_slayer, spectra‚Üê
> flawless_reign, luna‚Üêwarrior_of_light, zulgath‚Üêhoard_lord; **nocturna's unlock is still
> pending** ‚Äî see ¬ß41 ach-nocturna-unlock). The 5 newer companions don't have their own ¬ß
> sections yet; treat `companions.js` as the source of truth for the roster.

> Persistent in-HUD succubus companion who reacts to everything the player does and everything that happens in the dungeon, delivers the tutorials, and breaks the fourth wall. Bottom-left peeking portrait + RPG chat bubble. Personality: flirty + wicked with a sarcastic/sinister edge. 42 hand-drawn expression sprites. Data-driven line bank. Hideable via a 3-way Off/Quiet/Normal option. Source sprites: `D:\Documents\Game Jam Code\Quest-Failed assets\Main NPC` (42 PNGs).

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |

Locked companions still render at full size ‚Äî silhouette-tinted portrait with a padlock badge ‚Äî so the player sees the character teased but not their dialogue / personality. First locked companion: **Nocturna** (moonlit cat-girl witch, idle portrait only ‚Äî full implementation deferred). Source art: `Quest-Failed assets/Main NPC 5 - Nocturna`.

## 41. Achievements (2026-05-25)

> **Reconciled 2026-05-31:** `achievements.json` now holds **92** achievements (34 progression ¬∑
> 20 combat ¬∑ 4 economy ¬∑ 18 variety ¬∑ 16 mastery), not the 45 quoted below. Reward unlocks:
> **9 boss** + **5 companion** (hoard_lord‚Üízulgath, curtain_call‚Üírattlebones,
> flawless_reign‚Üíspectra, monarch_slayer‚Üínecroknight, warrior_of_light‚Üíluna) + titles. The
> "45" text below is the historical count at launch of the system.

> 45-achievement progression layer surfacing milestones + gating content unlocks. Reachable from the main menu + from per-row chips on the leaderboard (Phase C). Boss-level achievements (lvl 1‚Äì20) cover most of the slots; 25 non-level achievements span onboarding ‚Üí mastery. Hoard Lord (10k gold in one run) unlocks Zul'Gath, who's now locked at first-boot.

| Item | Description | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| ach-data | `src/data/achievements.json` ‚Äî 45 declarative entries with id, name, description, category, metric, target, optional reward { type, id }, icon glyph | 41 | ‚úÖ DONE | 27 progression + 5 combat + 2 economy + 6 variety + 5 mastery. 9 boss rewards (lvl 2‚Äì10 ‚Üí Golem ‚Ä¶ Slime), 1 companion reward (Hoard Lord ‚Üí Zul'Gath), 35 pure recognition. |
| ach-system | `src/systems/AchievementSystem.js` ‚Äî runtime engine. Prevents the ToastQueue's MAX_TOASTS=4 cap from silently dropping retro-unlocks when a long-time player first boots into the new system | 41 | ‚úÖ DONE | E.g., a player at maxBossLevel = 10 first-booting now sees 10 boss-level achievements unlock in a staggered cascade over ~7 seconds, each with its own toast, instead of all 10 firing in one tick and losing 6 of them. |

| ach-visual-polish | Visual polish pass after user feedback that the overlay was "way too much yellow." Five sub-changes landed together: (A) per-category color tokens (`--qf-cat-progression` amber, `--qf-cat-combat` blood-pink, `--qf-cat-economy` gold, `--qf-cat-variety` cyan, `--qf-cat-mastery` violet) drive icon, card border, glow, name color, and a subtle 4-5% card-bg tint per category ‚Äî the grid now reads as color bands rather than a wall of gold; (B) reward-chip semantics ‚Äî boss-unlock chips render oxblood (`--qf-reward-boss`), companion-unlock chips render rose (`--qf-reward-companion`), title-grant chips render violet (`--qf-reward-title`) via `data-reward-type` on the chip; (C) subtle card-bg tint via `color-mix(... 4-5%, var(--bg-1))` per category so even at a defocused glance the grid reads as bands; (D) title-chip inherits its source achievement's category color via `data-source-cat` (e.g. "The Hoarder" ‚Üí gold, "The Hunter" ‚Üí cyan, "The Tyrant" ‚Üí amber); (E) legendary tier ‚Äî six hand-picked endgame achievements (`throne_eternal`, `endless_reign`, `hoard_lord`, `veteran_exterminator`, `boss_slayer`, `class_hunter`) get a showcase treatment via `data-legendary="true"`: persistent inner ember glow, slow pulse, linear-gradient shimmer-sweep across the card, gold-bright accent. Plus icon variety ‚Äî every achievement now has a thematic glyph in `achievements.json` (no more 28 cards showing the same ‚ñ≤ triangle): boss-rewards use thematic per-boss glyphs (Lich ‚òÝ, Orc ‚öî, Vampire ‚ôÝ, Wraith ‚òæ, Succubus ‚ôÄ, etc.), boss-level 11-20 escalate through star variants (‚òÖ ‚ú™ ‚ú´ ‚ú¨ ‚ú≠ ‚úÆ ‚úØ ‚ú∞ ‚òº ‚ùÇ), pinnacle achievements use regal glyphs (‚ôï Endless Reign, ‚ôõ Boss Slayer). Category-tab active state also adopts the per-category color when filtered. Gold is now reserved for: economy color, the LEADERBOARD CTA, the run counter | 41 | ‚úÖ DONE | CSS-only change for most of the work ‚Äî only minimal JS in AchievementsOverlay for the data-attrs + a `LEGENDARY_IDS` Set + title source-cat lookup via `AchievementSystem.getDefinition`. The mango cheat's "everything unlocked" state now reads as a rich tapestry instead of a gold sea ‚Äî the original user complaint that drove this pass. Subsequent iteration: each card got `padding-right: 56px` on the text col to reserve space for the absolute-positioned rarity badge so the name never reads as cut-off; reward chip got `white-space: nowrap; max-width: 100%; text-overflow: ellipsis` so longer chips don't break layout; name color flipped from category-tinted back to parchment cream `#ece2d2` with a subtle category-tinted shadow so each card only has ONE focal point (the icon medal) instead of three competing same-color elements; icon set switched to thematic emoji (‚ö° ‚åõ ‚òÝ ‚öî ü¶é üçÑ üßõ üëª üíã üíß üëë etc.) with `U+FE0F` variation selectors forcing emoji presentation on glyphs that default to monochrome text. |

## Solo Leveling event ‚Äî Shadow Monarch (back-documented 2026-05-28)

The rare Shadow Monarch invader ("Sung Jinwoo") and his bespoke duel. The base feature shipped earlier without coverage rows; recorded here alongside the epic-duel cinematic overhaul.

| id | item | phase | status | notes |

Rolls organically in the rotation as of 2026-05-28 (`_eventPrecondMet` no longer gates it off) |
| sl-requeue | **If the boss DIES to Solo Leveling (Jinwoo wins the duel), the event is thrown back into the pool ‚Äî recurs without waiting for the full roster to cycle** | SL P6 | ‚úÖ DONE | `_onDayPhaseEnded`: when `id==='solo_leveling'` && `boss._diedThisDay`, don't add it to `firedThisRun` + drop any stale entry, so the shuffle bag keeps it eligible. Jinwoo losing ‚Üí marked spent normally |
| sl-aura | Persistent blue‚Üîblack cycling flame aura + glow on Jinwoo; shadow minions get the matched cycled flame; flame extinguishes on a shadow's death | SL P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | AdventurerRenderer `_attachShadowMonarchAura` + per-frame lerp tint; MinionRenderer shadow flame cycle + death removal |

## Light Party event ‚Äî FFXIV Trinity Raid (added 2026-05-29)

A 4-role coordinated raid party (Tank/Healer/DPS/DPS) inspired by FFXIV light party gameplay. Always exactly 4 members ‚Äî stat scaling per boss level keeps the encounter threatening at any era without changing the count. **Held out of the random shuffle bag** until the user opts to enable it (`_eventPrecondMet` exclusion); dev TEST EVENT button still force-fires it for QA.

| id | item | phase | status | notes |
|----|------|-------|--------|-------|
| lp-event | `light_party` event (`eventTier: 'boss'`, `colorTheme: 'lightparty'`) ‚Äî sweeping white‚Üígold‚Üísky-blue banner, gold boss-tier overlay automatic | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | events.json entry; EventBanner `_ensureLightPartyBannerCss` mirrors shadowmonarch pattern. **Held out of shuffle bag** via `_eventPrecondMet` until user enables; dev force-fire still works |
| lp-classes | 4 new adventurer classes (paladin / white_mage / samurai / black_mage), event-only `unlockLevel: 99`, dedicated LPC sprite sets (50 variants each + atk overlays) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | adventurerClasses.json; `tools/lpc-pools.mjs` per-class POOLS (paladin = plate+shield, white_mage = robes+staff+crystal, samurai = Saber katana proxy, black_mage = wizard hat + staff); baked to `assets/sprites/adventurers/<class>/v01..v50.png` + `_atk.png` via `bake-lpc-variants.mjs` + `bake-weapons.cjs`; FFXIV-flavored last words + chat lines |
| lp-spawn | Wave override: always spawn the fixed 4-member roster (Tank/Healer/2√óDPS) with role flags + shared partyId; replaces the normal day's wave entirely | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | DayPhase `_spawnLightParty`; wave-preview label "LIGHT PARTY" |
| lp-requeue | If the boss DIES to a Light Party duel (party wins), event is thrown back into the shuffle bag (mirrors Solo Leveling) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | EventSystem `_onDayPhaseEnded` extends the solo_leveling re-queue rule with `lightPartyBossDied` |
| lp-role-tank | Paladin Provoke aura ‚Äî minions within 4 tiles re-target the tank instead of squishier party members | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | MinionAISystem `_pickTarget` post-process: if best target is a non-tank Light Party member AND a tank within 4 tiles, swap. + Hallowed Ground (3s invuln at <30% HP, once per dungeon) in LightPartyAi |
| lp-role-healer | White Mage never attacks ‚Äî heals lowest-HP ally every 1.5s; on any party-member death starts a 3s interruptable Raise cast (>15% maxHp damage cancels); successful raise revives at 50% HP | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | CombatSystem `_neverAttacks` short-circuit (generic); LightPartyAi `_tickHealing` + `_tickRaiseCasts`; visible heal beam + cast bar via LightPartyRenderer |
| lp-role-dps | Samurai (2√ó ATK melee) + Black Mage (2√ó ATK ranged, attackRange 4 ‚Äî shoots over the tank); same trinity tradeoff feel | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | adventurerClasses.json stat tuning; standard AISystem combat (no special branch needed beyond per-class baseStats) |
| lp-lb-gauge | Shared LB gauge (0‚Äì100) fills from damage taken (0.5pt per 1% maxHp), minion kills (5pt), successful raises (10pt) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | EventSystem `_onLightPartyHit` / `_onLightPartyMinionKill` / `_onLightPartyRaise` + `_bumpLbGauge`; emits `LIGHT_PARTY_LB_GAUGE` for the corner-panel HUD |
| lp-lb-tactical | Tactical LB fires in the dungeon at full gauge ‚Äî Tank LB "Stronghold" (4s party invuln at <50% party HP); Healer LB "Pulse of Life" (full revive + heal when ‚â•2 dead); DPS LB "Final Heaven" (5-tile AoE kill when ‚â•4 minions in range) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | LightPartyAi `_tickLimitBreaks` priority dispatch + per-LB fire methods; screen flash + banner via LightPartyCinematic; `_invuln` flag respected by CombatSystem |
| lp-cinematic-entrance | Entrance card on spawn (‚óÜ LIGHT PARTY ‚óÜ / WARRIORS OF LIGHT / role chips fading in one-by-one) + persistent gold vignette | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | LightPartyCinematic `_playEntrance` + `_startVignette` (self-injected CSS) |
| lp-corner-panel | Persistent FFXIV party-list corner panel ‚Äî 4/8 stacked HP bars with role icons + LB gauge below; lifts when duel begins | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | LightPartyCinematic `_buildCornerPanel`; HP feed via AISystem `LIGHT_PARTY_HP` throttle (10Hz) |
| lp-world-vfx | World-space visuals: job icons hovering over heads (üõ° ‚ú® ‚öî üèπ), heal beam from healer to ally, raise cast bar over healer head | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | LightPartyRenderer (Phaser primitives, separate from AdventurerRenderer); tears down on DUEL_BEGAN + DAY_PHASE_ENDED |
| lp-duel | FFXIV-style cinematic boss fight ‚Äî letterbox bars, boss HP top, party HP list bottom-left, boss cast bar; 8-beat scripted sequence (opener ‚Üí AoE cast ‚Üí AoE resolve ‚Üí heal phase ‚Üí stack cast ‚Üí stack resolve ‚Üí LB3 climax ‚Üí resolution) over 17s | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | BossSystem `_runLightPartyDuel` + `_scriptLightPartyDuel`; LightPartyCinematic `_onDuelBegan` / `_onDuelBeat` / `_onDuelCast` / `_onDuelHp` / `_onDuelEnd`; outcome rolled at start from `0.25 + healerHpFrac*0.55 + livingDps*0.05 ‚àí (tankDead ? 0.15 : 0)`, clamped [0.10, 0.90] |
| lp-duel-bookkeeping | Win = boss loses a life (`deathsRemaining--`, `_diedThisDay=true`); Loss = party wipes via `_killAdv` (graveyard entries fire normally) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | BossSystem `_resolveLightPartyDuel`; emits BOSS_FIGHT_RESOLVED + LIGHT_PARTY_DEFEATED_BOSS (on win) + LIGHT_PARTY_DUEL_END (always); final-death gate via existing BOSS_DEFEATED_FINAL path |
| lp-achievement | Legendary 'warrior_of_light' ‚Äî granted when the BOSS wins the duel (party defeated by the dungeon). Reward: Luna companion + "Warrior of Light" title (titleFx `lightparty`, white‚Üígold‚Üísky-blue sweep) | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | achievements.json `warrior_of_light` + `metric: lightPartyDefeated`; AchievementSystem `_onLightPartyDuelEnd` (loss ‚Üí latch 1); bit-order entry; CSS `.qf-titlefx-lightparty` |
| lp-luna-unlock | Luna companion unlock ‚Äî flips `locked: true` on achievement grant via existing `PlayerProfile.unlockCompanion` path | LP P1 | ‚úÖ DONE | Reuses the same reward.type==='companion' wiring as monarch_slayer ‚Üí necroknight; Luna already had stub entry + idle portrait baked, so no companions.js change needed |

## The Kingdom's Reckoning ‚Äî act-based run structure & win condition (added 2026-05-31)

> See DESIGN.md ‚Üí "The Kingdom's Reckoning" for the full spec. The game's first **WIN condition**: a 4-act campaign (fixed Act I + IV, Acts II/III **drafted** from an 8-deep Kingdom Responses pool weighted **adaptively**) with a recurring **Nemesis** throughline, per-act **boss evolution**, and a **victory ‚Üí meta-unlock ‚Üí Endless** handoff. Design locked 2026-05-31; **build not started ‚Äî all ‚è≥ PENDING.** Build order: KR P1 ‚Üí P2 ‚Üí P3 (playable vertical slice) ‚Üí P4‚ÄìP5 (variety) ‚Üí P6‚ÄìP7 (payoff).

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|

Verified live. |

Fixed acts (I survival, IV duel) ungated. Feedback: urgent "THE CHAMPION STILL STANDS" flash + log beat. Verified: gate logic 5/5 cases + the banner renders. **Universal condition** (per 2026-06-01 design call ‚Äî every act = "defeat the Champion"); per-response theme twists deferred as polish. |

## AI & Personality Overhaul (added 2026-06-10) ‚Äî the deferred personality revamp + exploration "theater"

> Full spec: DESIGN.md ‚Üí "Adventurer AI & Personality Overhaul (2026-06-10) ‚Äî VERBATIM SPEC".
> **Build not started ‚Äî all ‚è≥ PENDING.** Build order: Nerve spine ‚Üí Appraisal (+revive
> `decisionOverrides`) ‚Üí Party Social (+Confer) ‚Üí Enhancements B/C ‚Üí roster/data ‚Üí Enhancements
> D/E/F. **Tick each box against the actual code before claiming "done."** Numbers (nerve bands,
> drain/recover rates, confer cadence) are tunables ‚Äî settle in `sim`/preview, not up front.

| ai-appraise-score | Doorway appraisal: risk + reward score | ‚úÖ DONE (2026-06-10) | `AISystem._appraiseRoom(adv,room)` scores from the adv's OWN knowledge (per-adv `adv.knowledge` + `KnowledgeSystem.tierForEntry` tier-weighting ‚Äî NOT re-derived from sharedPool). Brief pause (`_appraisingUntil`, 220‚Äì620ms ‚Äî **watchdog-exempt** via stuckExempt + freeze gate, far under the 1.5s soft / 10s hard timers), then creep (`_creepUntil` slows pace) / peek-back (capped `APPRAISE_MAX_PEEKBACKS=2` ‚Üí TACTICAL_RETREAT) / enter. ---

## How to keep this file honest

- **At every phase exit**: update statuses for items tagged in that phase. If a row is still PENDING or PARTIAL when the phase ends, either fix it or get explicit user approval to defer.
- **When the user adds new design items**: add them here with phase + status before implementing.
- **Open-ended (üí≠) items**: track running counts in the relevant section (e.g. "12/30 mechanics shipped").
- **When implementation differs from design**: don't silently rewrite this file ‚Äî flag the divergence to the user and update DESIGN.md if they approve.

---
